It's so tempting to substitute test counts for observation, conversation, and thinking. Reducing everything to bare numbers allows fabulous efficiency because of all the things we can just assume without having to hear them. And of course this creates a reservoir of lies by omission. It's so easy to lie by allowing your listener to continue making false assumptions about what you're doing.

昆虫节

Bugfests

我们已经看到 bugfests 如何给人一种错误的进步感。大量的猴子敲击大量的键并不能构成测试效率的有效衡量标准，而只是另一种欺骗管理者的方式，让他们认为已经完成了很多工作。另外，如果你发现了很多bug，是测试有效还是产品不好？

We're already seen how bugfests can give a false sense of progress. Lots of monkeys banging lots of keys does not constitute an effective measure of testing efficacy, but is merely another way to scam managers into thinking a great deal has been accomplished. Besides, if you find a great many bugs, does that mean the testing is effective or the product is lousy?

不要将非测试视为测试。

Don't count non-tests as tests.

听起来很神奇，测试人员有时会试图通过声称非测试与测试相同来欺骗他们的经理，如以下骗局所示：

Amazing as it sounds, testers sometimes try to scam their managers by claiming that a non-test is the same as a test, as the following scams illustrate:

什么都没有改变的骗局

The Nothing's-Changed Scam

声称“没有测试等于测试”的典型例子是“我们已经测试过了，没有任何改变”。这转化为“……什么都没有改变（我能想到的）”。而且，当然，正是那些您没有想到的更改导致了大多数新引入的错误。

The classic example of claiming "no testing equals testing" is the statement, "We already tested that, and nothing's changed." This translates into ". . . nothing's changed (that I can think of)." And, of course, it's those changes you don't think of that cause most of the newly introduced bugs.

一样的骗局

The It's-the-Same-Thing Scam

同一主题的一个细微变化是声明，“我已经测试了 X，它与 Y 相同，所以我不需要测试 Y”。我记得一个代价高昂的错误，当时测试人员声称从 CD 加载系统与从磁盘驱动器加载系统是一样的。也许它应该是，但事实并非如此。这就是我们进行测试的原因——看看应该为真的东西是否真的是真的。在这种情况下，所有运送给客户的 CD 都必须召回，因为它们无法正确加载。

A slight variation on the same theme is the statement, "I already tested X, and it's the same as Y, so I don't need to test Y." I remember a very costly mistake when a tester claimed that loading a system from a CD was the same thing as loading it from a disk drive. Maybe it should have been, but it wasn't. That's why we test—to see whether what should be true actually is true. In this case, all the CDs shipped to customers had to be recalled because they wouldn't load correctly.

部分测试作为一个完整的测试骗局

The Partial-Test-As-a-Complete-Test Scam

当测试人员将部分测试解释为完整测试并说“是的，我测试了表中的所有值”时，就会出现另一种常见的自犯骗局。（毕竟，测试人员测试了第一个值、第二个值、中间值和最后一个值。这等于同一件事，不是吗？）

Yet another common self-perpetrated scam arises when the tester interprets a partial test as a complete test, saying, "Yes, I tested all the values in the table." (After all, the tester tested the first value, the second value, a value in the middle, and the last value. That amounts to the same thing, doesn't it?)

整洁得令人难以置信。

It's too tidy to be true.

想象如下场景：Carlos 和 Paul 正在查看他们最新的测试报告。“读起来​​很有趣，”卡洛斯说。“看看这些图表。整齐。漂亮。教科书质量，甚至。” “唔。” 卡洛斯越过保罗的肩膀看着图表。“我明白你的意思了。很好奇。让我们问问泰瑞，她从哪里弄来的。”

Imagine a scene like the following: Carlos and Paul are looking over their latest test report. "It's an interesting read," Carlos says. "Look at these graphs. Tidy. Nice. Textbook-quality, even." "Hmm." Carlos peers over Paul's shoulder at the graphs. "I see what you mean. Curious. Let's ask Teri where she got them."

他们发现泰瑞正要离开办公室去开会。保罗举着图表。“这只需要一分钟。我们想知道你是如何创建这些图表的。”

They catch Teri about to leave her office for a meeting. Paul holds up the charts. "This will just take a minute. We were wondering how you created these graphs."

“用电子表格。” 泰瑞的表情出卖了她对这样一个问题的困惑。

"With a spreadsheet." Teri's expression betrays her puzzlement at such a question.

“没有。我们的意思是，数据是从哪里来的？” 卡洛斯问道。“你是如何衡量测试工作量的？你是如何使错误发现和关闭曲线如此平滑的？”

"No. We mean, where did the data come from?" Carlos asks. "How did you measure the test effort? How did you make the bug-find-and-close curves so smooth?"

“哦，那个。管理层坚持要我提交一份测试报告，但我们没有收集任何数据。我尽力估计如果我们保持跟踪的话这些数字会是多少。”

"Oh, that. Management insisted I turn in a test report, but we hadn't been gathering any of the data. I did my best to estimate what the numbers would have been if we'd kept track."

幸运的是，Carlos 和 Paul 知道不要被过于整洁、过于整齐、过于完美的数据所吸引。真实数据永远不会那么整洁。

Fortunately, Carlos and Paul know better than to be suckered by data that are too neat, too tidy, too perfect. Real data are never that neat.

排列在电子表格中的垃圾仍然是垃圾。

Garbage arranged in a spreadsheet is still garbage.

不幸的是，卡洛斯和保罗的管理层中了泰瑞无意的骗局。它将她的测试报告作为所有其他测试经理应该制作的那种报告的示例。他们还将 Teri 的电子表格作为模板分发给所有其他测试人员使用。他们不仅为 The Tidiness Scam 上当，还为 The Spreadsheet Scam 上当：如果它来自电子表格，它一定是正确的。

Unfortunately, Carlos and Paul's management fell for Teri's unintentional scam. It held up her test report as an example to all other test managers of the kind of report they should be producing. They also distributed Teri's spreadsheet as a template for all the other testers to use. They fell not just for The Tidiness Scam, but also for The Spreadsheet Scam: If it comes from a spreadsheet, it must be right.

与任何其他计算机程序一样，电子表格具有垃圾进垃圾出的特性。不然怎么可能呢？

A spreadsheet, like any other computer program, exhibits the garbage-in-garbage-out property. How could it be otherwise?

概括

Summary

当我们非常希望一切顺利时，很容易将我们的幻想注入我们的数据中。

When we want so much for everything to go well, it's all too easy to inject our fantasies into our data.

常见错误

Common Mistakes

1.使用已交付产品的早期错误报告来估计已交付错误总数：在早期，用户尚未探索产品的全部功能，不常用的功能可能更容易出现错误。

1. Using early reports of errors from a shipped product to estimate total errors shipped: Early on, users haven't yet explored the full functionality of a product, and less-frequently-used features may be more likely to have bugs.

2.使错误报告变得乏味或不便：测试报告会被任何不鼓励立即记录发现的错误的东西所扭曲。

2. Making bug reporting tedious or inconvenient: Test reports will be distorted by anything that discourages immediate recording of found bugs.

3.创造一个鼓励伪造测试报告的指责环境：你永远不应该因为别人的信息内容而惩罚他们，不管这些信息对你来说多么不愉快。要了解有关责备环境的更多信息，请参阅“超越责备：大型系统开发项目中的一致性”。[18]

3. Creating a blaming environment that encourages falsified test reporting: You should never punish people for the content of their messages, no matter how unpleasant the message may be for you. To learn more about blaming environments, see "Beyond Blaming: Congruence in Large Systems Development Projects." [18]

4.形式重于内容：报告整洁固然很好，但最重要的是，报告应该及时准确。

4. Rewarding form over content: It's nice if reports are neat, but first and foremost, reports should be timely and accurate.

5.奖励数量而不是质量：如果你奖励忙碌，你会得到很多测试，但测试不多。

5. Rewarding quantity over quality: If you reward busyness, you'll get lots of tests, but not much testing.

结语

Epilogue

 

“美国公众在剧院里想要的是一个圆满结局的悲剧。” - William Dean Howells，美国作家和文学评论家（1837-1920），引用自 Edith Wharton，A Backward Glance: An Autobiography （纽约：Scribner，1998）。

"What the American public wants in the theater is a tragedy with a happy ending." - William Dean Howells, American Author and Literary Critic (1837–1920), as quoted in Edith Wharton, A Backward Glance: An Autobiography (New York: Scribner, 1998).

如果您对软件测试的所有困难感到灰心，我想给您一个圆满的结局。那可能吗？

If you're feeling discouraged by all the difficulties of software testing, I'd like to give you a happy ending. Is that possible?

如果您是那些对完美无懈可击的人感到满意的人，就不可能有圆满的结局。这个世界上没有完美，所以对你来说没有幸福。

A happy ending won't be possible if you're one of those people who will be happy with nothing short of perfection. There can be no perfection in this world, so for you there can be no happiness.

但如果你更现实一点，那么，是的，有很多幸福的结局。为何如此？好吧，软件测试的故事并不是真正的悲剧。这是一个关于我们努力超越人性弱点的故事。如果你把软件测试中的情况看成一个过程，而不是一个状态，那么当然实际上不会有结局，但过程有可能是快乐的。

But if you're of a more realistic bent, then, yes, there are numerous happy endings. How so? Well, the story of software testing isn't really a tragedy. It's a story of our struggles to transcend our all-too-human frailties. If you look at the situation in software testing as a process, not a state, then of course there won't actually be an ending, but the process has a chance of being happy.

为了让这个过程愉快，我们可能不得不放慢我们的雄心壮志，让软件构建的艺术赶上来。我们可能必须改进我们的测试实践，以使我们的工作达到我们所知的最佳水平。当我们接近计划的项目结束时，我们肯定必须控制那些往往会淹没我们的知识和逻辑的情绪。

For the process to be happy, we may have to slow down our ambitions a bit to allow the art of software-building to catch up. We may have to improve our testing practices to bring our work up to the best we know. And we will definitely have to master those emotions that tend to overwhelm our knowledge and logic as we near the scheduled end of our projects.

但是，如果我们接受挑战去做这些困难的事情，那么下一个半个世纪的软件开发肯定会继续我们在过去半个世纪中看到的惊人进步。你可以指望它。

But if we take up the challenge to do these difficult things, then the next half-century of software development will certainly continue the astonishing progress we've seen over the past half-century. You can count on it.

尾注

Endnotes

 

[1] 有关此主题的更多信息，请参阅 GM Weinberg 的《计算机编程心理学：二十周年纪念版》（纽约：多塞特出版社，1998 年）。测试大师 James Bach 断言我已经写了一本关于测试的书，他说：“当然不止一本——也许你所有的书都是测试书。通用系统思维导论就是关于如何穿透周围的幻想技术。它是关于如何接近、操纵、观察和思考系统的。它不被视为一本测试书，主要是因为你没有称它为测试书，而且因为你没有做太多展示软件示例的事情在其中进行测试。我想这很重要，但除其他外，您的职业和工作主体一直都与测试有关。”

[1] See G.M. Weinberg, The Psychology of Computer Programming: Silver Anniversary Edition (New York: Dorset House Publishing, 1998) for more on this topic. Master tester James Bach asserts that I have already written a book about testing, saying "More than one, of course—perhaps all of your books have been testing books. An Introduction to General Systems Thinking is all about how to penetrate the illusions that surround technology. It's about how to approach and manipulate and observe and think about systems. It is not seen as a testing book, mostly because you didn't call it a testing book, and because you didn't do much to show examples of software testing within it. That's important, I guess, but still, your career and body of work have been all about testing, among other things."

 

 

[2] 有关我对这些问题的更多思考，请参阅质量软件管理：卷。2、First-Order Measurement（纽约：Dorset House Publishing，1993）。

[2] For more on my thinking on these issues, see Quality Software Management: Vol. 2, First-Order Measurement (New York: Dorset House Publishing, 1993).

[3] For techniques on spotting and using all information, see the four volumes of Quality Software Management (New York: Dorset House Publishing, Vol. 1, 1992; Vol. 2, 1993; Vol. 3, 1994; and Vol. 4, 1997). Volume 1 has now been replaced by the two volumes: How Software is Built (2010) and Why Software Gets In Trouble (2010)

[4] First published in 1975, An Introduction to General Systems Thinking: Silver Anniversary Edition (New York: Dorset House Publishing, 2001) explores aspects of nonlinear systems thinking.

 

 

[5] 参见 Tom F. Crum，《冲突的魔力》（纽约：Touchstone，Simon & Schuster，1987 年）。Gerald M. Weinberg 在 Gerald M. Weinberg 的More Secrets of Consulting（纽约：Dorset House Publishing，2002 年），p.中进一步发展了幻想作为现实的概念。34ff。

[5] See Tom F. Crum, The Magic of Conflict (New York: Touchstone, Simon & Schuster, 1987). The concept of fantasy as reality is further developed in Gerald M. Weinberg, More Secrets of Consulting (New York: Dorset House Publishing, 2002), p. 34ff.

 

 

[6] Gerald M. Weinberg 在 Gerald M. Weinberg 的More Secrets of Consulting（纽约：Dorset House Publishing，2002 年）中进一步探讨了完整信息不言而喻的想法以及发现缺失元素的方法。130ff。另见 GM Weinberg，咨询的秘密（纽约：Dorset House Publishing，1985 年），p。84.

[6] The idea of the full message going unspoken—and ways to discover the missing element—is further explored in Gerald M. Weinberg, More Secrets of Consulting (New York: Dorset House Publishing, 2002), p. 130ff. See also G.M. Weinberg, The Secrets of Consulting (New York: Dorset House Publishing, 1985), p. 84.

 

 

[7] 开发人员和程序员似乎为自己能够解决失败的问题而感到自豪。有关来自各行各业的示例，请参见 Gerald M. Weinberg，咨询的秘密（纽约：多塞特出版社，1985 年），第 43-45 页。

[7] Developers and programmers seem to take pride in their ability to make features of their failures. For examples taken from all walks of life, see Gerald M. Weinberg, The Secrets of Consulting (New York: Dorset House Publishing, 1985), pp. 43–45.

 

 

[8] 期望这个主题非常重要，因此我不想在本书的背景下处理它，而是建议您参考许多人认为是权威的著作。参见 Naomi Karten，Managing Expectations（纽约：Dorset House Publishing，1994 年）。

[8] The subject of expectations is so important that rather than try to treat it within the context of this book, I refer you to what many consider to be the definitive work. See Naomi Karten, Managing Expectations (New York: Dorset House Publishing, 1994).

 

 

[9] 每个人迟早都必须学会这一课的价值：“把钱放在嘴边。” 有关该主题的更多信息，请参阅 Gerald M. Weinberg，咨询的秘密（纽约：Dorset House Publishing，1985 年），第 135-36 页。

[10] 参见 William E. Perry 和 Randall W. Rice，在软件测试的十大挑战中幸存下来：一种以人为本的方法（纽约：Dorset House Publishing，1997）。

[11] 即使是简单的单词也会妨碍有效的沟通。有关此主题的更多信息，请参阅http://www.ayeconference.com/Articles/LullabyLanguage.html。另见 GM Weinberg，更多咨询的秘密（纽约：Dorset House Publishing，2002 年），p。27ff。

[11] Even simple words can get in the way of effective communication. For more on this topic, see http://www.ayeconference.com/Articles/LullabyLanguage.html. See also G.M. Weinberg, More Secrets of Consulting (New York: Dorset House Publishing, 2002), p. 27ff.

 

 

[12] 软件项目中的模式主题长期以来一直吸引着 IT 行业。有关综合处理，请参阅 Gerald M. Weinberg，质量软件管理，Vols。1–4（纽约：Dorset House Publishing，1992–97）。要深入了解模式识别如何成为引导项目走向失败或成功的关键，请参阅 Tom DeMarco 等人的Adrenaline Junkies and Template Zombies（纽约：Dorset House Publishing，2008 年）。

[12] The topic of patterns in software projects has long absorbed the IT industry. For a comprehensive treatment, see Gerald M. Weinberg, Quality Software Management, Vols. 1–4 (New York: Dorset House Publishing, 1992–97). For a compelling look at how pattern recognition can be key to steering a project toward failure or success, see Tom DeMarco et al., Adrenaline Junkies and Template Zombies (New York: Dorset House Publishing, 2008).

 

 

[13] 战争故事在 Cem Kaner、James Bach 和 Bret Pettichord 的《软件测试中的经验教训：上下文驱动方法》（纽约：John Wiley & Sons，2001 年）中敏锐地说明了这一点。

[13] War stories keenly illustrate this point in Cem Kaner, James Bach, and Bret Pettichord, Lessons Learned in Software Testing: A Context-Driven Approach (New York: John Wiley & Sons, 2001).

 

 

[14] 詹姆斯·巴赫 (James Bach) 在 2007 年夏天的某个时间阅读了我手稿草稿中的这些材料后，问我是否记得很久以前的断言，“不应忘记在编码时考虑测试的教训。可能没有任何一种测试技术是比远见更有价值。” 这些词出现在Computer Programming Fundamentals, 2nd ed的第 377 页。（纽约：McGraw-Hill，1966 年），这是我与合著者 Herb Leeds 合写的一本书。James 刚刚发现了这本书：“我把这本书放在我面前，因为它在 [William] Hetzel 1973 年的书 Program Test Methods中被引用，作为编程书籍只提供令人沮丧的测试建议的规则的一个例外。你的书是在我出生的那年出版。我现在才开始阅读它。”

[14] James Bach, after reading this material in my manuscript draft sometime during the summer of 2007, asked me whether I remember long ago asserting, "The lesson of considering testing when coding should not be forgotten. Probably no single testing technique is of more value than foresight." These words appear on page 377 of Computer Programming Fundamentals, 2nd ed. (New York: McGraw-Hill, 1966), a book I wrote with coauthor Herb Leeds. James was just discovering the book: "I have this open in front of me because it was cited in [William] Hetzel's 1973 book, Program Test Methods, as an exception to the rule that programming books provided only dismal testing advice. Your book was published the year I was born. I'm only now getting around to reading it."

嗯，我的记忆力不是很好，所以我不记得那些确切的词，但至少我没有忘记原理。那时我们确实知道一些重要的事情，但每一代人都必须自己去发现它们。

Well, my memory isn't that good, so I don't remember those exact words, but at least I haven't forgotten the principle. We did know a few important things back then, but each generation has to discover them for itself.

[15] For comprehensive details both on getting stakeholders and on running technical reviews, see Daniel P. Freedman and Gerald M. Weinberg, Handbook of Walkthroughs, Inspections, and Technical Reviews, 3rd ed. (New York: Dorset House Publishing, 1990).

 

 

[16] 要了解如何量化“不可量化”，请参阅质量软件管理：卷。2、First-Order Measurement（纽约：Dorset House Publishing，1993）。

[16] To learn about quantifying the "unquantifiable," see Quality Software Management: Vol. 2, First-Order Measurement (New York: Dorset House Publishing, 1993).

 

 

[17] 有关完整的故事和其他可以让您热血沸腾的故事，请参阅 Cem Kaner、James Bach 和 Bret Pettichord，Lessons Learned in Software Testing：A Context-Driven Approach（纽约：John Wiley & Sons，2001 年）。

[17] For the full story and others that will get your blood circulating, see Cem Kaner, James Bach, and Bret Pettichord, Lessons Learned in Software Testing: A Context-Driven Approach (New York: John Wiley & Sons, 2001).

 

 

[18] 对于这篇我与家庭治疗师和 Satir 研究所负责人 Jean McLendon 合着的文章，请参阅“Beyond Blaming：Congruence in Large Systems Development Projects”，IEEE Software， Vol。13，第 4 期（1996 年），第 33-42 页。该文章也可在线访问 http://www.ayeconference.com/Articles/BeyondBlaming.html。

The article is also available online at http://www.ayeconference.com/Articles/BeyondBlaming.html.

补充阅读

Additional Reading

 

对于那些希望继续探索软件测试世界的人，我推荐以下所有内容。

For those who wish to continue with their exploration of the world of software testing, I recommend all of the following.

 

 

贝泽尔，鲍里斯。

Beizer, Boris.

软件测试技术，第 2 版。

Software Testing Techniques, 2nd ed.

纽约：Van Nostrand Reinhold，1990 年。

New York: Van Nostrand Reinhold, 1990.

软件测试人员的教科书，涵盖了截至出版之日的几乎所有技术问题。通过软件测试中的经验教训，它涵盖了传统的激进软件测试智慧的两端。

A textbook for software testers, covering pretty much all the technical issues as of the date of publication. With Lessons Learned in Software Testing, it covers both ends of the conventional-radical software-testing wisdom.

 

 

科普兰，李。\

Copeland, Lee. \

软件测试设计从业者指南。

A Practitioner's Guide to Software Test Design.

波士顿：Artech House，2004 年。

Boston: Artech House, 2004.

这是一本极好的参考书或教科书，提供了最常见测试方法的可靠概述。

This is an excellent reference or textbook providing a solid overview of the most common test methods.

 

 

Kaner、Cem、James Bach 和 Bret Pettichord。

Kaner, Cem, James Bach, and Bret Pettichord.

软件测试中的经验教训：上下文驱动的方法。

Lessons Learned in Software Testing: A Context-Driven Approach.

纽约：John Wiley & Sons，2002 年。

New York: John Wiley & Sons, 2002.

测试人员和管理人员积累的大量智慧，来自测试人员中的三盏灯。它不是教科书，也不是一口气读完，而是放在你的办公桌上，每天至少拿起一次，随意打开，学习有用的技巧，提高你的工作绩效。

Lots of accumulated wisdom for testers and managers, from three leading lights among testers. It is not a textbook, and not to be read at one sitting, but keep it on your desk and pick it up at least once a day, and open at random to learn a useful tip that will improve your job performance.

 

 

Perry、William E. 和 Randall W. Rice。

Perry, William E., and Randall W. Rice.

克服软件测试的十大挑战：以人为本的方法。

Surviving the Top Ten Challenges of Software Testing: A People-Oriented Approach.

纽约：多赛特出版社，1997 年。

New York: Dorset House Publishing, 1997.

本书简短、甜美、切中要点，强调了软件测试中许多最重要的人为问题。

Short, sweet, and to the point, this book highlights many of the most important human issues in software testing.

 

 

最后一个建议：在过去的几年里，我一直在教授软件原理，包括测试，通过写激动人心的虚构故事来展示这些课程，而不仅仅是告诉他们。我的 Smashwords 作者页面列出了我所有的小说以及示例章节以帮助您在其中进行选择。< http://www.smashwords.com/profile/view/JerryWeinberg >

One final recommendation: Over the past few years, I've been approaching the teaching of software principles, including testing, by writing exciting fictional stories showing these lessons, not just telling them.My Smashwords author page has a listing of all my novels as well as sample chapters to help you choose among them. <http://www.smashwords.com/profile/view/JerryWeinberg>

如果您喜欢平装书，请查看我在 Amazon.com < http://www.amazon.com/-/e/B000AP8TZ8 >和其他书商网站上的作者页面。或者询问您当地的书商是否可以为您获取它们。我想当你从我的小说中学到一些东西时，你会喜欢我的小说。感谢您试一试。

If you prefer paperbound books, check my author page on Amazon.com <http://www.amazon.com/-/e/B000AP8TZ8> and other booksellers' websites. Or ask your local bookseller about obtaining them for you. I think you'll enjoy my novels while you're learning a few things from them. Thanks for giving them a try.
